`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/OffsetAndMetadata.java` - Used by consumers to track committed offsets\\n- **Server-side**: `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetAndMetadata.java` - Server representation of committed offsets with epoch information\\n\\nThese classes store the committed offset, optional metadata string, commit timestamp, and optional expiration timestamp.\\n\\n### 2. **GroupCoordinator Offset Commit Handler**\\n\\nThe offset commit workflow is orchestrated through:\\n- **GroupCoordinator Interface**: `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.java` - Defines commitOffsets, fetchOffsets, and deleteOffsets contract\\n- **GroupCoordinatorService**: `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorService.java` - Implements the coordinator interface with commitOffsets method\\n- **GroupCoordinatorShard**: `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorShard.java` - Handles per-shard offset commit operations\\n\\n### 3. **OffsetFetch Request Processor**\\n\\nOffset fetching is handled through request/response classes:\\n- **OffsetFetchRequest**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetFetchRequest.java` - Client request to fetch committed offsets\\n- **OffsetFetchResponse**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetFetchResponse.java` - Server response with offset data\\n- **OffsetMetadataManager**: `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManager.java` - Core manager implementing fetchOffsets logic\\n\\n### 4. **Offset Commit Management**\\n\\nOffset commit operations are implemented through:\\n- **OffsetCommitRequest**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetCommitRequest.java`\\n- **OffsetCommitResponse**: handled through:\\n- **OffsetDeleteRequest**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetDeleteRequest.java`\\n- **OffsetMetadataManager.deleteOffsets()**: Deletion
